simplify automated translation between any languages, transformation and mutation of texts/code/messages in any language and so on.\n\nSo we need to be able to fully support storage (presenting as So widest possible range of operations for any language via the prism of meta language will be supported.\n\nWe should check that nothing is defered or left unimplemented in our vision and roadmap. When corrupted or non-image files, such as GitHub \"Not Found\" pages saved as `.png`, are read, they can cause \"Could not process image\" errors and crash the AI solver process. ## Filed sub-issues (#49–#63)

All 15 specs were filed, attached as sub-issues of #47 via the `sub_issues` API, and blocked-by relations wired via the native issue-dependencies API:

- Phase 1 (parallel): #49 readonly/mutable engine, #50 format grammars, #51 programming-language grammar wave, #52 pluggable parser registry, #53 LiNo network serialization, #56 natural-language grammar parsing, #57 exact-match shared concept space, #60 query/transform algebra, #61 incremental re-parse + structural sharing
- Phase 2: #54 doublets binary storage (blocked by #49, #53), #55 Rust types↔links codec (#53), #58 translation-rule registry (#52, #57)
- Phase 3: #59 language restriction profiles (#58), #62 API-style parity contract (#54, #58)
- Phase 4 (closing gate): #63 competitor corpora wave 2 + coverage ratchet (#50, #56, #60, #62)

Per issue #47's instruction, every sub-issue states that its work lands on this branch (`issue-47-76af108c0f24`) and merges through this PR.
